# Changelog

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

# Changelog

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

## 1.0.0 (2025-12-23)

* fix: Add missing dependencies and configuration parameters ([2136d2b](https://github.com/hamidedefr/MPtoO-v2/commit/2136d2b))

# Changelog

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

## 1.0.0 (2025-12-22)

* fix: Add missing dependencies and configuration parameters ([2136d2b](https://github.com/hamidedefr/MPtoO-v2/commit/2136d2b))

and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

# Changelog

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

# Changelog

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

# Changelog

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

# Changelog

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

All notable changes to MPtoO will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).
